## Analysis

The Ground Truth (GT) is:
$$-0.19494483384724354 \cdot A + 0.24819026785686927 \cdot \cos(\log(A + 1))$$

Let me check the candidates systematically.

**Candidate 48:** `A*c0 + c1 + c2*sin(c3*log(A*c4 + 1) + c5)`

This can be written as: $c_0 \cdot A + c_1 + c_2 \cdot \sin(c_3 \cdot \log(c_4 \cdot A + 1) + c_5)$

Using the identity $\cos(\theta) = \sin(\theta + \pi/2)$, we can write:
$$\cos(\log(A+1)) = \sin(\log(A+1) + \pi/2)$$

Setting:
- $c_0 = -0.19494483384724354$
- $c_1 = 0$
- $c_2 = 0.24819026785686927$
- $c_3 = 1$ (coefficient of log)
- $c_4 = 1$ (so $\log(1 \cdot A + 1) = \log(A+1)$)
- $c_5 = \pi/2$

This gives: $-0.19494 \cdot A + 0 + 0.24819 \cdot \sin(\log(A+1) + \pi/2) = -0.19494 \cdot A + 0.24819 \cdot \cos(\log(A+1))$

This matches the GT exactly! ✓

**Candidate 127:** `c0 + c1*cos(c2*log(A*c3 + 1))`

Setting $c_0 = 0$, $c_1 = 0.24819$, $c_2 = 1$, $c_3 = 1$ gives $0.24819 \cdot \cos(\log(A+1))$, but this lacks the $-0.19494 \cdot A$ term and has no way to produce it. ✗

**Candidate 80:** `A**c0*c1 + c2 + c3*sin(c4*log(A*c5 + 1) + c6)`

Setting $c_0 = 1$, $c_1 = -0.19494$, $c_2 = 0$, $c_3 = 0.24819$, $c_4 = 1$, $c_5 = 1$, $c_6 = \pi/2$:

This gives: $-0.19494 \cdot A + 0 + 0.24819 \cdot \sin(\log(A+1) + \pi/2) = -0.19494 \cdot A + 0.24819 \cdot \cos(\log(A+1))$

This also matches! ✓

**Candidate 9:** `c0 + c1*exp(A*c2) + c3*sin(c4*log(A*c5 + 1) + c6)`
